    SELECT [o].[Id], [o].[Carrier], [o].[OrderDate], [o].[ShippingAddress], [o].[Status], [o].[TotalAmount], [o].[TrackingNumber], [o].[TransactionId], [o].[UserId]
    FROM [Orders] AS [o]
    ORDER BY [o].[OrderDate] DESC
    OFFSET @p ROWS FETCH NEXT @p1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [o1]
LEFT JOIN [OrderItems] AS [o0] ON [o1].[Id] = [o0].[OrderId]
ORDER BY [o1].[OrderDate] DESC, [o1].[Id]
